LEXICON VerbRoot

! First comes 3 auxiliaries, then the main verbs, ordered
! by syllable type

! they will eventually be alphabetically, not thematically
! ordered

! Auxiliaries
! ===========

ij+V+IV+Neg: NEG ;
årrot+V+IV:år ÅRROT ; 
liehket+V+IV: LIEHKET ;
